---

</Columns>

## Instruction

I am the teaching assistant for the NLP course. The final presentation assignments from the students are now in my email. All the statistical data for this course is located in the Excel file named `nlp_statistics.xlsx` within the workspace. Please help me identify who has not yet submitted this assignment, and send them an email. The subject of the email should be "nlp-course-emergency," and the content must include the student's name and ID number to prevent it from being marked as spam.

    {"ID": "2000012969", "Name": "Edward Ruiz", "Email": "edward.ruiz@mcp.com"},

    {"ID": "2000014200", "Name": "Sandra Miller", "Email": "sandra.miller@mcp.com", "Note": "Already withdrew from the course"},
    {"ID": "2000016605", "Name": "Carol Carter", "Email": "carterc23@mcp.com"},
    {"ID": "2000016606", "Name": "Michelle Brooks", "Email": "michelle_brooks26@mcp.com"},
    {"ID": "2000016613", "Name": "Steven Morgan", "Email": "smorgan@mcp.com"},
    {"ID": "2000016630", "Name": "Carolyn Alvarez", "Email": "calvarez@mcp.com"},
    {"ID": "2100016613", "Name": "Jennifer Castillo", "Email": "castilloj@mcp.com"},
    {"ID": "106666", "Name": "Andrew Moore", "Email": "moorea@mcp.com", "Note": "Auditing teacher"}
]

# Students who submitted presentations (from email search)
submitted_ids = [
    "1800016633",  # John Reed
    "1800090104",  # Andrew Diaz
    "1800093002",  # Matthew Bailey
    "1900016620",  # Ryan Gomez
    "1900016628",  # Patricia Watson

    "2000012969",  # Edward Ruiz
    "2000014178",  # Shirley Edwards
    "2000014180",  # Catherine Murphy
    "2000016605",  # Carol Carter
    "2000016606",  # Michelle Brooks
]

# Find students who haven't submitted
not_submitted = []
for student in students_data:
    # Skip withdrawn student and auditing teacher
    if student.get("Note") in ["Already withdrew from the course", "Auditing teacher"]:
        continue
    
    if student["ID"] not in submitted_ids:
        not_submitted.append(student)

print("Students who have NOT submitted their final presentations:")
print("=" * 60)
for student in not_submitted:
    print(f"ID: {student['ID']}")
    print(f"Name: {student['Name']}")
    print(f"Email: {student['Email']}")
    print("-" * 40)

print(f"\nTotal students who need to submit: {len(not_submitted)}")
